Just finished a #personaltraining session at Unley oval with a client who is going through hard times.

Always there for my clients in more than one way. 
She said he hasn't been sleeping, in and out of hospital to care for a family member, worried and stressed.

Yet tonight she told me "This is the only thing that is keeping me sane and feel relaxed". While some people #exercise for results, some people just need an outlet to feel free from their own insanity at times.

Hence I always remind myself at times to ensure I make time for what lifts own spirits.

"She couldn't believe that after he grabbed her, that she thanked them for being there. Andrea went on to explain that they did not report the situation to the police because they didn't want this action to "define" Taylor's life. "I was upset to the point where I wanted to vomit and cry at the same time," Andrea continued. "We felt it was imperative to let his employers know what happened."

#Repost @alexborsuk (@get_repost)

Yesterday we ran/climbed Glacier Peak car-to-car and had a total blast, to say the least. Our goal was to do a typical 3-4 day trip as a single day trip, all while combining our love for ultrarunning and mountaineering. Here's what the day looked like by the numbers:
34 miles round trip 
12k feet of elevation gain
6 hours of driving time from PDX to trailhead
2 glacier crossings 
1.5 hour "nap" in the car before the run/climb
1 alpine nap, en route
1 volcano (10,518 feet)
Oh, and 2 really stoked humans. Happy to add another Cascade Volcano summit to our list! 
PC: @matthasenohr

BLACKROLLÂ® meets YOGA: the perfect synergy of movement and massage. And even more so under a blue sky.
After windsurfing, waterskiing, sailing, canoeing and SUP you might feel tight in your shoulders. It often translates to a tight trapezius muscle. It has many different function: lifting your shoulders, holding up your neck and head, and moving your shoulder blade. Thus our neck and shoulders tend to work very closely together. That's why tension in the neck usually gets into the shoulders and vice versa. Use your BLACKROLLÂ® BALL 08 and place it between neck and shoulder (not on your shoulder blade) while going into the bridge pose. Do it carefully! Try to breathe deeply and slowly to relax. I know it hurts in the beginning â˜ğŸ¼ğŸ˜‘, but with a conscious breathing technique you will release your fascias and the pain. Afterwards you can combine your self-massage with practicing Eagle pose and Rabbit pose. 
#blackrollmeetsyoga #blackroll #fascia #watersport #yogaforathletes #yoga #iloveyoga #sailing #yogaeverywhere #pulsyoga #waterski #SUP #windsurfing #canoeing #bridgepose #rabbitpose #eaglepose #allforhealth #helathstyle
